    2754           8 : TEST(crs, scope_area_bbox_remark) {
    2755             :     auto in_wkt = "GEODETICCRS[\"JGD2000\","
    2756             :                   "DATUM[\"Japanese Geodetic Datum 2000\","
    2757             :                   "  ELLIPSOID[\"GRS 1980\",6378137,298.257222101]],"
    2758             :                   "CS[Cartesian,3],"
    2759             :                   "  AXIS[\"(X)\",geocentricX],"
    2760             :                   "  AXIS[\"(Y)\",geocentricY],"
    2761             :                   "  AXIS[\"(Z)\",geocentricZ],"
    2762             :                   "  LENGTHUNIT[\"metre\",1.0],"
    2763             :                   "SCOPE[\"Geodesy, topographic mapping and cadastre\"],"
    2764             :                   "AREA[\"Japan\"],"
    2765             :                   "BBOX[17.09,122.38,46.05,157.64],"
    2766             :                   "VERTICALEXTENT[-10000,10000],"
    2767             :                   "TIMEEXTENT[2002-04-01,2011-10-21],"
    2768             :                   "ID[\"EPSG\",4946],\n"
    2769             :                   "REMARK[\"some_remark\"]]";
    2770             :     auto crs =
    2771           2 :         nn_dynamic_pointer_cast<GeodeticCRS>(WKTParser().createFromWKT(in_wkt));
    2772           2 :     ASSERT_TRUE(crs != nullptr);
    2773             : 
    2774           5 :     ASSERT_EQ(crs->domains().size(), 1U);
    2775           1 :     auto domain = crs->domains()[0];
    2776           3 :     EXPECT_TRUE(domain->scope().has_value());
    2777           3 :     EXPECT_EQ(*(domain->scope()), "Geodesy, topographic mapping and cadastre");
    2778           3 :     ASSERT_TRUE(domain->domainOfValidity() != nullptr);
    2779           4 :     EXPECT_TRUE(domain->domainOfValidity()->description().has_value());
    2780           4 :     EXPECT_EQ(*(domain->domainOfValidity()->description()), "Japan");
    2781           6 :     ASSERT_EQ(domain->domainOfValidity()->geographicElements().size(), 1U);
    2782           2 :     auto geogElement = domain->domainOfValidity()->geographicElements()[0];
    2783           1 :     auto bbox = nn_dynamic_pointer_cast<GeographicBoundingBox>(geogElement);
    2784           2 :     ASSERT_TRUE(bbox != nullptr);
    2785           4 :     EXPECT_EQ(bbox->southBoundLatitude(), 17.09);
    2786           4 :     EXPECT_EQ(bbox->westBoundLongitude(), 122.38);
    2787           4 :     EXPECT_EQ(bbox->northBoundLatitude(), 46.05);
    2788           4 :     EXPECT_EQ(bbox->eastBoundLongitude(), 157.64);
    2789             : 
    2790           6 :     ASSERT_EQ(domain->domainOfValidity()->verticalElements().size(), 1U);
    2791           2 :     auto verticalElement = domain->domainOfValidity()->verticalElements()[0];
